{"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01EoKH2PBHAboFVPPWDGekv4","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_01PLgjiS9y6nAVwt4v7LHUvX","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/documentation.md","content":"# Envoy Connection Pool Management Troubleshooting Runbook\n\n## 1. Architecture Overview\n\n### Connection Pool Organization\n\nEnvoy connection pools manage upstream connections on a **per-cluster, per-thread basis**. Each Envoy worker thread maintains its own pool of connections for each upstream cluster, ensuring thread-safe operation without locks.\n\n#### Pool Structure\n\nConnection pools maintain four lists of active clients:\n- **`ready_clients_`**: Connections in `Ready` state (can accept new streams immediately)\n- **`busy_clients_`**: Connections at concurrent stream limit or draining\n- **`connecting_clients_`**: Connections still establishing TCP/TLS handshake\n- **`early_data_clients_`** (HTTP/3): Connections with 0-RTT credentials ready for early data\n\nPending streams waiting for available connections are held in:\n- **`pending_streams_`**: Queue of requests waiting for a connection to become available\n\n**Source**: `source/common/conn_pool/conn_pool_base.h:376-388`\n\n### Connection Lifecycle\n\nA connection progresses through the following states:\n\n```\nConnecting → Ready ──┬─→ Busy (at concurrent stream limit)\n                      │\n                      └─→ Draining (no more streams accepted, close after active streams finish)\n                           │\n                           └─→ Closed (queued for deletion)\n```\n\n**State Definitions**:\n- **Connecting**: TCP/TLS handshake in progress, `connect_timeout` applies\n- **ReadyForEarlyData** (HTTP/3 only): Ready to accept 0-RTT streams\n- **Ready**: Can accept additional streams immediately\n- **Busy**: Reached `max_concurrent_streams` limit (HTTP/2) or processing a stream (HTTP/1.1)\n- **Draining**: Received GOAWAY or circuit breaker triggered; closes after active streams complete\n- **Closed**: Connection destroyed, object deferred-deleted\n\n**Source**: `source/common/conn_pool/conn_pool_base.h:89-98`\n\n### HTTP/1.1 vs HTTP/2 Connection Differences\n\n#### HTTP/1.1 Pools\n- **One stream per connection** (multiplexing not supported)\n- `numActiveStreams()` returns 1 or 0 based on stream wrapper presence\n- Connection returns to `Ready` state only after stream completes (headers + body received)\n- State: `Connecting` → `Ready` → `Busy` (during stream) → `Ready` → `Draining`\n\n**Source**: `source/common/http/http1/conn_pool.h:28-34`\n\n#### HTTP/2 Pools\n- **Multiple streams per connection** (multiplexing)\n- `max_concurrent_streams` negotiated via HTTP/2 SETTINGS frame (can adjust after connection established)\n- Connection can accept new streams until concurrent stream limit reached\n- Sends GOAWAY to gracefully drain; actively transitions to `Draining` state\n- Receives peer SETTINGS; adjusts `concurrent_stream_limit_` down if needed\n\n**Source**: `source/common/http/conn_pool_base.cc:111-150` (onGoAway, onSettings handlers)\n\n### Per-Connection Configuration Limits\n\nEach active connection respects:\n- **`max_concurrent_streams`** (HTTP/2): Negotiated in handshake + SETTINGS updates\n- **`max_requests_per_connection`** (global): `host->cluster().maxRequestsPerConnection()`\n- **`remaining_streams_`**: Decrements with each stream; connection closes when 0 (or per-connection-buffer-limit reached)\n\n**Source**: `source/common/conn_pool/conn_pool_base.h:125-138`\n\n---\n\n## 2. Common Failure Scenarios\n\n### Scenario 1: Connection Pool Exhaustion (Pending Requests Overflow)\n\n**Symptom**: Clients see 503 errors; Envoy logs contain `\"max pending streams overflow\"`\n\n**Metrics to Check**:\n- `upstream_cx_overflow_` counter: Number of requests rejected due to pending overflow\n- `circuit_breakers.<cluster_name>.<priority>.cx_open_` gauge: Circuit breaker open (1 = open)\n- `circuit_breakers.<cluster_name>.<priority>.remaining_pending_` gauge: Remaining pending request capacity\n- `upstream_rq_pending_active_` gauge: Current pending streams in pool\n\n**Root Cause Analysis**:\n\nThis occurs when the number of in-flight requests exceeds `circuit_breakers.thresholds[].max_pending_requests`. The pool cannot create new connections fast enough or connections cannot drain pending requests quickly.\n\n```\nRequest arrives → Pool checks: canCreate(pending_requests)?\n                              ↓ No (at limit)\n                   → onPoolFailure(Overflow)\n                   → Reject request (503 + circuit_breaker_exceeded)\n```\n\n**Code Location**: `source/common/conn_pool/conn_pool_base.cc:346-350`\n\n**Diagnostic Steps**:\n\n1. **Check pending request circuit breaker status**:\n   ```bash\n   curl http://localhost:9901/stats/prometheus | grep 'circuit_breakers.*remaining_pending'\n   ```\n   Expected output (if open): `remaining_pending 0`\n\n2. **Check active pending streams**:\n   ```bash\n   curl http://localhost:9901/stats/prometheus | grep 'upstream_rq_pending_active'\n   ```\n   High value indicates backlog.\n\n3. **Examine cluster configuration**:\n   ```bash\n   curl http://localhost:9901/clusters | grep -A 20 '<cluster_name>'\n   ```\n   Look for `circuit_breakers` section, specifically `max_pending_requests`.\n\n4. **Check upstream response times** (slow backend):\n   ```bash\n   curl http://localhost:9901/stats/prometheus | grep 'upstream_rq_time'\n   ```\n   If `upstream_rq_time` histogram shows high latencies (mean/p99 >> 100ms), backend is slow.\n\n5. **Check for connection creation failures**:\n   ```bash\n   curl http://localhost:9901/stats/prometheus | grep 'upstream_cx_connect'\n   ```\n   High `upstream_cx_connect_fail` or `upstream_cx_connect_timeout` indicates cannot establish connections fast enough.\n\n**Configuration Fixes**:\n\n**Option A: Increase max_pending_requests**\n```yaml\nclusters:\n- name: my-cluster\n  circuit_breakers:\n    thresholds:\n    - priority: DEFAULT\n      max_pending_requests: 2048  # Increase from default 1024\n```\n⚠️ **Only if**: Temporary traffic spike; backend can handle more load.\n\n**Option B: Increase max_connections**\n```yaml\nclusters:\n- name: my-cluster\n  circuit_breakers:\n    thresholds:\n    - priority: DEFAULT\n      max_connections: 512  # Increase from default 100-200\n```\n- More connections = more concurrency; scales pending request handling.\n- Monitor resource consumption (memory, file descriptors).\n\n**Option C: Enable connection preconnection**\n```yaml\nclusters:\n- name: my-cluster\n  preconnect_policy:\n    num_initial_connections: 10\n    num_retries: 3\n```\n- Pre-establishes connections before requests arrive.\n- Reduces latency of new streams; mitigates pending overflow.\n\n**Option D: Reduce upstream latency**\n- Add caching at downstream proxy layer.\n- Optimize backend handler (database queries, external API calls).\n- Scale backend horizontally.\n\n---\n\n### Scenario 2: Upstream Connection Reset / Premature Close\n\n**Symptom**: Intermittent 503 errors; logs show `RemoteClose` or `LocalClose` events; high `upstream_cx_*` churn\n\n**Metrics to Check**:\n- `upstream_cx_total_` counter: Total connections created (high value = churn)\n- `upstream_cx_connect_fail_` counter: Failed connection attempts (TCP RST, refused)\n- `upstream_cx_rx_bytes_buffered_` vs `upstream_cx_rx_bytes_total_`: Data buffered/received\n- `upstream_rq_per_cx_` histogram: Requests per connection (low = short-lived)\n\n**Root Cause Analysis**:\n\nUpstream actively closes connections or connections fail before requests complete:\n\n1. **Backend resets TCP connection** (RST flag):\n   - Load balancer/firewall closing idle connections\n   - Backend overload (OOM, resource exhaustion)\n   - Connection timeout or keepalive expiry\n\n2. **TLS handshake failures**:\n   - Certificate validation errors\n   - TLS version mismatch\n   - SNI mismatch\n\n3. **HTTP/2 protocol violations**:\n   - Invalid HEADERS or DATA frames\n   - Stream ID exhaustion (rare)\n\n**Code Paths**:\n- `ActiveClient::onEvent(Network::ConnectionEvent::RemoteClose)` → `PoolFailureReason::RemoteConnectionFailure`\n- `ActiveClient::onEvent(Network::ConnectionEvent::LocalClose)` → `PoolFailureReason::LocalConnectionFailure`\n\n**Source**: `source/common/conn_pool/conn_pool_base.cc` and `source/common/tcp/conn_pool.cc:84-100`\n\n**Diagnostic Steps**:\n\n1. **Check connection count and failures**:\n   ```bash\n   curl http://localhost:9901/stats/prometheus | grep -E 'upstream_cx_(total|connect_fail|close|reset)'\n   ```\n   Interpret:\n   - `upstream_cx_total > 1000` per minute = high churn\n   - `upstream_cx_connect_fail / upstream_cx_total > 5%` = connection issues\n\n2. **Check TCP connection state**:\n   ```bash\n   # On proxy box, monitor upstream connections\n   netstat -antp | grep -E '<upstream_ip>:80|443' | wc -l\n   # Compare with expected (max_connections setting)\n   ```\n\n3. **Check for idle timeout on upstream**:\n   ```bash\n   # If seeing many connections but few requests, upstream likely closing idle\n   curl http://localhost:9901/stats/prometheus | grep 'upstream_rq_per_cx'\n   # Low values (1-2) suggest connections closing quickly\n   ```\n\n4. **Check Envoy's connection timeout configuration**:\n   ```bash\n   curl http://localhost:9901/config_dump | jq '.configs[] | select(.config_type==\"Cluster\")' | grep -E 'connect_timeout|tcp_keepalives'\n   ```\n\n5. **Check for TLS errors** (if using HTTPS upstream):\n   ```bash\n   tail -f /var/log/envoy/access.log | grep -i 'ssl\\|tls\\|certificate'\n   # Or check Envoy debug logs at WARN level\n   ```\n\n**Configuration Fixes**:\n\n**Option A: Increase connect_timeout (if TLS handshake slow)**\n```yaml\nclusters:\n- name: my-cluster\n  connect_timeout: 10s  # Default is 1s; increase for slow links\n```\n\n**Option B: Enable TCP keepalive**\n```yaml\nclusters:\n- name: my-cluster\n  upstream_connection_options:\n    tcp_keepalives:\n      keepalive_probes: 3\n      keepalive_interval: 10s\n      keepalive_time: 60s\n```\n- Prevents OS from closing idle TCP connections\n- Upstream sees regular keepalive packets\n\n**Option C: Disable per-connection request limit** (if requests per connection very low)\n```yaml\nclusters:\n- name: my-cluster\n  max_requests_per_connection: 0  # Unlimited\n  # or high value: 10000\n```\nConnections reuse for many requests.\n\n**Option D: Adjust pool idle timeout** (for TCP pools)\n```yaml\nclusters:\n- name: my-cluster\n  tcp_pool_idle_timeout: 10s  # Default likely higher\n```\nClose idle TCP connections proactively to reduce resource usage.\n\n**Option E: Check upstream load balancer settings**\n- Increase backend's `tcp_tw_reuse` (TIME_WAIT recycling)\n- Increase backend's max file descriptor limit\n- Check if upstream is actively rejecting connections (`netstat -s | grep 'rejected'`)\n\n---\n\n### Scenario 3: Circuit Breaker Triggering Unexpectedly\n\n**Symptom**: Large portion of traffic returning 503; circuit breaker stats show `cx_open_` = 1; no obvious upstream issues\n\n**Metrics to Check**:\n- `circuit_breakers.<cluster>.<priority>.cx_open_` : 1 = open, 0 = closed\n- `circuit_breakers.<cluster>.<priority>.remaining_*` gauges (connections, pending_requests, requests)\n- `upstream_cx_total_` : total connections (should equal `max_connections` if breaker open)\n\n**Root Cause Analysis**:\n\nThe resource manager prevents new connections/requests before the pool actually reaches capacity. This can happen due to:\n\n1. **Transient traffic spike**: Spike exceeds threshold momentarily\n2. **Misconfigured limits**: `max_connections` set too low for actual traffic\n3. **Slow backend**: Connections held open longer; new requests blocked\n4. **Asymmetric configuration**: Multiple Envoy proxies competing for shared upstream; each proxy's limit too low\n\n**Code Flow**:\n```\nnewStream() called\n  → parent.host().resourceManager().pendingRequests().canCreate()?\n  → if No: onPoolFailure(Overflow, ...) // Not ConnectionFailure\n```\n\n**Source**: `source/common/conn_pool/conn_pool_base.cc:346-350`\n\n**Diagnostic Steps**:\n\n1. **Confirm circuit breaker is actually open**:\n   ```bash\n   curl http://localhost:9901/stats/prometheus | grep 'circuit_breakers.*\\.cx_open_' | grep ' 1$'\n   # If > 0, breaker is open\n   ```\n\n2. **Check remaining capacity**:\n   ```bash\n   curl http://localhost:9901/stats/prometheus | grep 'remaining_' | grep 'circuit'\n   # Look for remaining_connections_*, remaining_pending_*\n   # If 0, threshold reached\n   ```\n\n3. **Check current vs max**:\n   ```bash\n   # Get max_connections setting\n   curl http://localhost:9901/clusters | grep -A 30 '<cluster_name>' | grep -i 'max.*connection'\n\n   # Count current active connections\n   curl http://localhost:9901/stats/prometheus | grep 'upstream_cx_total'\n   ```\n   If `upstream_cx_total >= max_connections`: Expected behavior, breaker should open.\n\n4. **Check if traffic pattern changed**:\n   ```bash\n   # Look at request rate and latency\n   curl http://localhost:9901/stats/prometheus | grep 'upstream_rq_' | grep -E '(time|total)'\n   ```\n\n5. **Check for slow requests**:\n   ```bash\n   # High mean/p99 latency = requests held longer = fewer concurrent capacity\n   curl http://localhost:9901/stats/prometheus | grep 'upstream_rq_time'\n   ```\n\n**Configuration Fixes**:\n\n**Option A: Increase max_connections**\n```yaml\nclusters:\n- name: my-cluster\n  circuit_breakers:\n    thresholds:\n    - priority: DEFAULT\n      max_connections: 512  # Increase from, e.g., 100\n```\nMust be balanced with resource (memory, file descriptors, RAM per host).\n\n**Option B: Increase per-host limits** (if using load balancing with multiple hosts)\n```yaml\nclusters:\n- name: my-cluster\n  common_http_protocol_options:\n    max_connections_per_host: 50  # Distribute connections across hosts\n  circuit_breakers:\n    thresholds:\n    - priority: DEFAULT\n      max_connections: 200  # Lower global limit OK if spread per-host\n```\n\n**Option C: Reduce request timeout**\n```yaml\nclusters:\n- name: my-cluster\n  timeout: 5s  # Shorter timeout = requests complete faster = more capacity\n```\nOnly if requests can realistically complete in time.\n\n**Option D: Add retries with exponential backoff** (at router level)\n```yaml\nvirtual_hosts:\n- name: my_vhost\n  routes:\n  - match:\n      prefix: /api\n    route:\n      cluster: my-cluster\n      retry_policy:\n        num_retries: 3\n        retry_host_predicate:\n        - name: envoy.retry_host_predicates.previous_hosts\n```\nAllows requests to retry against other backends if first attempt hits circuit breaker.\n\n**Option E: Monitor and alert on circuit breaker status**\n```yaml\n# Add metric watch\n# Alert when circuit_breakers.<cluster>.*.cx_open_ == 1 for > 10s\n```\n\n---\n\n### Scenario 4: HTTP/2 GOAWAY Causing Request Failures\n\n**Symptom**: Spike of 503 errors or stream resets; logs show upstream `GOAWAY` frame; requests fail with `RemoteReset` or `ConnectionTermination` reason\n\n**Metrics to Check**:\n- `upstream_cx_close_notify_` counter: Number of GOAWAY frames received\n- `upstream_rq_reset_` gauge: Active request resets\n- `upstream_rq_per_cx_` histogram: Drops sharply when GOAWAY sent\n\n**Root Cause Analysis**:\n\nHTTP/2 server sends GOAWAY frame when:\n1. **Graceful shutdown**: Server shutting down; tells clients to use other connections\n2. **Connection duration limit**: Server enforces max connection lifetime\n3. **Stream ID exhaustion**: Rare; 2^31 stream IDs consumed (millions of streams)\n4. **Protocol violation**: Invalid frame, stream reset, flow control violation\n5. **Resource constraint**: Memory pressure, too many streams\n\nWhen upstream sends GOAWAY:\n- All **in-flight streams on that connection are reset** (or complete if headers already sent)\n- Connection transitions to `Draining` state\n- No new streams assigned to connection\n- Connection closes after all active streams complete\n\n**Code Flow**:\n```cpp\nvoid MultiplexedActiveClientBase::onGoAway(Http::GoAwayErrorCode) {\n  // Line 112: Log debug message\n  // Line 113: Increment upstream_cx_close_notify_\n  if (numActiveRequests() == 0) {\n    close();  // No active streams, close immediately\n  } else {\n    transitionActiveClientState(*this, ActiveClient::State::Draining);  // Wait for streams to finish\n  }\n}\n```\n\n**Source**: `source/common/http/conn_pool_base.cc:111-121`\n\n**Diagnostic Steps**:\n\n1. **Confirm GOAWAY is being sent**:\n   ```bash\n   curl http://localhost:9901/stats/prometheus | grep 'upstream_cx_close_notify'\n   # If > 0, GOAWAYs are happening\n   ```\n\n2. **Timestamp of GOAWAY events**:\n   ```bash\n   # Tail envoy debug logs if available\n   tail -f /var/log/envoy/debug.log | grep -i 'goaway'\n   ```\n\n3. **Check active streams before/after**:\n   ```bash\n   # Monitor in real-time during incident\n   watch 'curl -s http://localhost:9901/stats/prometheus | grep -E \"upstream_cx|upstream_rq_active\"'\n   ```\n\n4. **Check upstream server logs for shutdown/scaling signals**:\n   ```bash\n   # On upstream service, check logs\n   tail -f /var/log/app/server.log | grep -i 'shutdown\\|drain\\|goaway'\n   ```\n\n5. **Check HTTP/2 settings negotiation**:\n   ```bash\n   curl http://localhost:9901/config_dump | jq '.configs[] | select(.config_type==\"Cluster\") | .config' | grep -i 'h2\\|http2'\n   ```\n\n**Configuration Fixes**:\n\n**Option A: Accept GOAWAY gracefully with retries**\n```yaml\n# At route level: enable retries to other connections/backends\nvirtual_hosts:\n- name: my_vhost\n  routes:\n  - match:\n      prefix: /\n    route:\n      cluster: my-cluster\n      retry_policy:\n        num_retries: 1\n        retry_on: reset  # Retry on connection reset/GOAWAY\n        per_try_timeout: 2s\n```\n\n**Option B: Reduce max_requests_per_connection** (if upstream has low limit)\n```yaml\nclusters:\n- name: my-cluster\n  max_requests_per_connection: 1000  # Gracefully close before upstream GOAWAY\n```\nPro-actively close Envoy-side connections to avoid GOAWAY surprise.\n\n**Option C: Increase idle timeout** (if upstream GOAWAYs idle connections)\n```yaml\nclusters:\n- name: my-cluster\n  http2_protocol_options:\n    connection_idle_timeout: 120s  # Increase from default\n```\n\n**Option D: Coordinate with upstream on shutdown**\n```yaml\n# Ensure upstream sends GOAWAY before accepting new connections\n# Document: \"When scaling down, send GOAWAY 30s before accepting no new connections\"\n# Envoy will move conn to Draining; backoff new streams to other upstream\n```\n\n**Option E: Monitor and alert**\n```yaml\n# Alert when upstream_cx_close_notify_ increases rapidly\n# Possible actions: auto-scale up downstream capacity, drain traffic to other upstreams\n```\n\n---\n\n## 3. Diagnostic Commands\n\n### Key Envoy Admin API Endpoints\n\n#### `/stats` (or `/stats/prometheus`)\nReturns all stats in Prometheus format. Useful for scripting.\n\n```bash\n# Get all connection pool stats for a cluster\ncurl http://localhost:9901/stats/prometheus | grep 'cluster\\.my_cluster'\n\n# Get circuit breaker status\ncurl http://localhost:9901/stats/prometheus | grep 'circuit_breaker'\n\n# Get HTTP/1 vs HTTP/2 specific metrics\ncurl http://localhost:9901/stats/prometheus | grep 'upstream_cx'\n```\n\n#### `/clusters`\nLists all clusters and their status (human-readable).\n\n```bash\ncurl http://localhost:9901/clusters | grep -A 30 'my_cluster'\n\n# Output includes:\n# - Circuit breakers thresholds\n# - Current connections\n# - Load balancer status\n# - Hosts/endpoints\n```\n\n#### `/config_dump`\nDumps the entire Envoy configuration (listeners, routes, clusters). JSON format.\n\n```bash\n# Dump cluster config\ncurl http://localhost:9901/config_dump | jq '.configs[] | select(.config_type==\"Cluster\") | select(.config.name==\"my_cluster\")'\n\n# Check circuit breaker config\ncurl http://localhost:9901/config_dump | jq '.configs[] | select(.config_type==\"Cluster\") | .config.circuit_breakers'\n```\n\n#### `/stats/histogram_bucket` (if available)\nBreaks down histogram values (e.g., `upstream_rq_time`) into buckets.\n\n```bash\ncurl http://localhost:9901/stats/histogram_bucket/upstream_rq_time\n```\n\n### Key Metrics for Connection Pool Diagnosis\n\n| Metric | Type | Meaning |\n|--------|------|---------|\n| `upstream_cx_total` | Counter | Total connections created |\n| `upstream_cx_overflow` | Counter | Connections rejected due to max circuit breaker |\n| `upstream_cx_connect_fail` | Counter | Failed TCP/TLS handshakes |\n| `upstream_cx_connect_timeout` | Counter | Connections timing out (exceed `connect_timeout`) |\n| `upstream_cx_close_notify` | Counter | Received GOAWAY (HTTP/2) or similar |\n| `upstream_rq_pending_total` | Counter | Total requests queued (ever) |\n| `upstream_rq_pending_active` | Gauge | Current pending requests |\n| `upstream_rq_per_cx` | Histogram | Requests completed per connection |\n| `upstream_rq_time` | Histogram | Request latency (downstream→upstream→downstream) |\n| `circuit_breakers.<cluster>.<priority>.cx_open_` | Gauge | 1 = circuit breaker open, 0 = closed |\n| `circuit_breakers.<cluster>.<priority>.remaining_*` | Gauge | Remaining capacity (connections, requests, pending) |\n\n### Example Diagnostic Session\n\n```bash\n# Step 1: Check overall cluster health\ncurl http://localhost:9901/clusters | grep my_cluster\n\n# Step 2: Check if circuit breaker is open\ncurl http://localhost:9901/stats/prometheus | grep 'circuit_breakers.*my_cluster.*cx_open'\n\n# Step 3: If open, check remaining capacity\ncurl http://localhost:9901/stats/prometheus | grep 'circuit_breakers.*my_cluster.*remaining'\n\n# Step 4: Check connection churn\ncurl http://localhost:9901/stats/prometheus | grep 'my_cluster.*upstream_cx_' | head -20\n\n# Step 5: Check request latency\ncurl http://localhost:9901/stats/prometheus | grep 'my_cluster.*upstream_rq_time'\n\n# Step 6: Dump config to verify settings\ncurl http://localhost:9901/config_dump | jq '.configs[] | select(.config.name==\"my_cluster\") | .config.circuit_breakers'\n```\n\n---\n\n## 4. Configuration Fixes and Tuning\n\n### Circuit Breaker Thresholds\n\n```yaml\nclusters:\n- name: my_cluster\n  circuit_breakers:\n    thresholds:\n    # DEFAULT priority (normal traffic)\n    - priority: DEFAULT\n      max_connections: 100\n      max_pending_requests: 100\n      max_requests: 100\n      max_retries: 3\n      track_remaining: true  # Export remaining_* stats\n    # HIGH priority (e.g., health checks, admin)\n    - priority: HIGH\n      max_connections: 10\n      max_pending_requests: 10\n      max_requests: 10\n      max_retries: 1\n```\n\n**Tuning Guidelines**:\n- **`max_connections`**: Typically `min(10, num_upstream_instances) * num_proxy_threads`\n  - If upstream has 4 instances and proxy has 8 worker threads: `10 * 8 = 80` per cluster\n  - Verify against resource limits (file descriptors, memory)\n- **`max_pending_requests`**: Usually `2–5x max_connections` to allow request queueing\n- **`max_requests`**: Usually same as `max_connections` to prevent overwhelming upstream\n- **`max_retries`**: Usually 3–5; may be 1 if retries happen at outer layer\n\n**Runtime Override** (for dynamic tuning):\n```yaml\n# In runtime_config.yaml or via runtime overrides\nruntime_values:\n  overrides:\n  - resource_key: \"circuit_breakers.my_cluster.default.max_connections\"\n    value: 200\n```\n\n### Connection Timeout and Keepalive\n\n```yaml\nclusters:\n- name: my_cluster\n  # TCP connection establishment timeout\n  connect_timeout: 2s  # Default 1s; increase for high-latency links (satellite, WAN)\n\n  # TCP keepalive for long-lived connections\n  upstream_connection_options:\n    tcp_keepalives:\n      keepalive_probes: 3         # TCP_KEEPCNT\n      keepalive_interval: 10s     # TCP_KEEPINTVL\n      keepalive_time: 300s        # TCP_KEEPIDLE (5 minutes)\n```\n\n**When to adjust**:\n- `connect_timeout > 1s`: When upstream is geographically distant or has slow TLS handshake\n- `tcp_keepalives`: When connections idle for extended periods; prevents intermediary (firewall, LB) from closing\n\n### Per-Connection Limits\n\n```yaml\nclusters:\n- name: my_cluster\n  # Max requests per connection before closing and opening new\n  max_requests_per_connection: 0  # 0 = unlimited (default); set to positive integer to limit\n\n  # HTTP/2 specific: max concurrent streams\n  http2_protocol_options:\n    max_concurrent_streams: 100   # Negotiated via SETTINGS frame\n    initial_stream_window_size: 65536  # Default 64KiB\n    initial_connection_window_size: 1048576  # Default 1MiB\n```\n\n**Tuning**:\n- `max_requests_per_connection`: Set to gracefully recycle connections (e.g., 10,000) if upstream has per-connection memory leaks\n- `max_concurrent_streams` (HTTP/2): If upstream advertises lower value, Envoy respects it. Override only if upstream value is too conservative.\n\n### Buffer Limits\n\n```yaml\nclusters:\n- name: my_cluster\n  # Max bytes buffered per upstream connection (for pending data)\n  per_connection_buffer_limit_bytes: 32768  # Default 32KiB\n\n  # Useful when upstream has slow write socket buffer or Envoy has memory constraints\n```\n\n**When to adjust**:\n- Decrease if proxying large request bodies and memory is limited\n- Increase if upstream has high RTT and benefits from buffering\n\n### Preconnection\n\n```yaml\nclusters:\n- name: my_cluster\n  preconnect_policy:\n    # Pre-establish N connections when pool is created\n    num_initial_connections: 5\n    # Number of additional connections to attempt if preconnect incomplete\n    num_retries: 3\n```\n\n**Effect**: Reduces latency of first request by pre-warming connection pool.\n\n### Example: High-Throughput Configuration\n\n```yaml\nclusters:\n- name: high_throughput_backend\n  connect_timeout: 3s  # TLS handshake can be slow\n\n  circuit_breakers:\n    thresholds:\n    - priority: DEFAULT\n      max_connections: 500  # Scale up for high throughput\n      max_pending_requests: 1000\n      max_requests: 500\n      max_retries: 5\n      track_remaining: true\n\n  http2_protocol_options:\n    max_concurrent_streams: 100\n    initial_connection_window_size: 2097152  # 2 MiB for large request bodies\n\n  upstream_connection_options:\n    tcp_keepalives:\n      keepalive_time: 60s\n      keepalive_interval: 10s\n      keepalive_probes: 3\n\n  max_requests_per_connection: 10000  # Recycle after 10k requests to prevent leaks\n\n  preconnect_policy:\n    num_initial_connections: 10\n    num_retries: 3\n```\n\n---\n\n## 5. Code References\n\n### Key Source Files and Functions\n\n#### Base Connection Pool (Shared Logic)\n- **File**: `source/common/conn_pool/conn_pool_base.h`\n  - `class ConnPoolImplBase`: Base pool implementation\n  - `class ActiveClient`: Base active connection representation\n  - `class PendingStream`: Queued request awaiting connection\n\n- **File**: `source/common/conn_pool/conn_pool_base.cc`\n  - `ConnPoolImplBase::newStreamImpl()`: Main entry point for new streams\n  - `ConnPoolImplBase::tryCreateNewConnections()`: Attempt to establish connections\n  - `ConnPoolImplBase::onConnectionEvent()`: Handle TCP/TLS events\n  - `PendingStream::PendingStream()`: Constructor; increments pending request count\n\n#### HTTP Connection Pool\n- **File**: `source/common/http/conn_pool_base.h`\n  - `class HttpConnPoolImplBase`: HTTP pool base (shared by HTTP/1.1 and HTTP/2)\n  - `class ActiveClient`: HTTP-specific active client\n  - `class MultiplexedActiveClientBase`: Base for HTTP/2 and HTTP/3 (multiplexed)\n\n- **File**: `source/common/http/conn_pool_base.cc`\n  - `MultiplexedActiveClientBase::onGoAway()`: **Handle HTTP/2 GOAWAY**\n  - `MultiplexedActiveClientBase::onSettings()`: **Handle HTTP/2 SETTINGS (max_concurrent_streams)**\n\n#### HTTP/1.1 Connection Pool\n- **File**: `source/common/http/http1/conn_pool.h`\n  - `class ActiveClient`: HTTP/1.1-specific active client\n  - `struct StreamWrapper`: Wraps request/response encoder/decoder pair\n\n- **File**: `source/common/http/http1/conn_pool.cc`\n  - HTTP/1.1 codec client instantiation\n\n#### HTTP/2 Connection Pool\n- **File**: `source/common/http/http2/conn_pool.h`\n  - `class ActiveClient`: HTTP/2-specific active client (inherits from `MultiplexedActiveClientBase`)\n\n- **File**: `source/common/http/http2/conn_pool.cc`\n  - HTTP/2 codec client instantiation\n  - SETTINGS frame handling\n\n#### TCP Connection Pool\n- **File**: `source/common/tcp/conn_pool.h`\n  - `class ConnPoolImpl`: TCP pool implementation\n  - `class ActiveTcpClient`: TCP active client\n\n- **File**: `source/common/tcp/conn_pool.cc`\n  - `ActiveTcpClient::onEvent()`: Handle TCP connection events\n  - `ActiveTcpClient::onIdleTimeout()`: Close idle TCP connections\n\n#### Circuit Breaker and Resource Management\n- **File**: `source/common/upstream/upstream_impl.h`\n  - `class ClusterInfoImpl::CircuitBreakerManager`: Manages resource thresholds\n\n- **File**: `source/common/upstream/upstream_impl.cc`\n  - `CircuitBreakerManager::CircuitBreakerManager()`: Initialize thresholds from config\n  - Resource increment/decrement logic\n\n### Tracing Pool Failures\n\nWhen diagnosing a pool failure, trace these code paths:\n\n**For Overflow (pending request rejected)**:\n1. `ConnPoolImplBase::newStreamImpl()` (line 259, base header)\n2. Check `resourceManager().pendingRequests().canCreate()` (upstream_impl.cc:347)\n3. Call `onPoolFailure(..., PoolFailureReason::Overflow, ...)` (upstream_impl.cc:349)\n\n**For Connection Failure (TCP RST/timeout)**:\n1. `ActiveClient::onEvent(Network::ConnectionEvent::RemoteClose)` or `LocalClose`\n2. Call `parent_.onConnectionEvent(*this, failureReason, event)` (conn_pool_base.cc:158)\n3. Call `onPoolFailure(..., PoolFailureReason::RemoteConnectionFailure/LocalConnectionFailure, ...)`\n\n**For HTTP/2 GOAWAY**:\n1. HTTP/2 codec receives GOAWAY frame\n2. Call `MultiplexedActiveClientBase::onGoAway(...)` (conn_pool_base.cc:111)\n3. Transition to `Draining` state (line 118)\n4. Drain remaining streams; close connection\n\n---\n\n## Appendix: Runtime Tuning Command Examples\n\n### Check Current Settings\n```bash\n# SSH to Envoy proxy\n$ ssh envoy-proxy.example.com\n\n# Query stats endpoint\n$ curl http://localhost:9901/clusters | grep -A 50 \"my_cluster\"\n$ curl http://localhost:9901/stats/prometheus | grep 'circuit_breakers.*my_cluster'\n```\n\n### Enable Debug Logging for Connection Pool\n```bash\n# At startup, set log level\nenvoy -l debug --config-path /etc/envoy.yaml\n\n# Or patch config at runtime (if admin API supports)\ncurl -X POST http://localhost:9901/logging?...  # Depends on Envoy version\n```\n\n### Monitor in Real-Time\n```bash\n# Watch pool stats every second\nwatch -n 1 \"curl -s http://localhost:9901/stats/prometheus | grep -E 'upstream_cx_|pending|circuit'\"\n\n# Or with jq for JSON prettification\nwatch -n 1 \"curl -s http://localhost:9901/config_dump | jq '.configs[] | select(.config_type==\\\"Cluster\\\") | select(.config.name==\\\"my_cluster\\\") | .config.circuit_breakers'\"\n```\n\n### Adjust Circuit Breaker via Config\nEdit `/etc/envoy/envoy.yaml`, update thresholds, and trigger config reload:\n```bash\n# HUP signal reloads config (graceful)\n$ kill -HUP $(pidof envoy)\n\n# Verify new settings applied\n$ curl http://localhost:9901/clusters | grep -A 50 \"my_cluster\"\n```\n\n---\n\n## Summary\n\nEnvoy connection pools are the critical path for upstream communication. Most production issues stem from:\n\n1. **Insufficient capacity** (circuit breakers too low)\n2. **Connection churn** (upstream closing, TLS failures, timeouts)\n3. **Slow backends** (pending request backlog)\n4. **Configuration mismatch** (Envoy limits vs. upstream capabilities)\n\nUse the diagnostic steps in **Section 3** to identify root cause, then apply fixes from **Sections 2 and 4**. Architecture Overview\n\n### Connection Pool Organization\n\nEnvoy connection pools manage upstream connections on a **per-cluster, per-thread basis**. Each Envoy worker thread maintains its own pool of connections for each upstream cluster, ensuring thread-safe operation without locks.\n\n#### Pool Structure\n\nConnection pools maintain four lists of active clients:\n- **`ready_clients_`**: Connections in `Ready` state (can accept new streams immediately)\n- **`busy_clients_`**: Connections at concurrent stream limit or draining\n- **`connecting_clients_`**: Connections still establishing TCP/TLS handshake\n- **`early_data_clients_`** (HTTP/3): Connections with 0-RTT credentials ready for early data\n\nPending streams waiting for available connections are held in:\n- **`pending_streams_`**: Queue of requests waiting for a connection to become available\n\n**Source**: `source/common/conn_pool/conn_pool_base.h:376-388`\n\n### Connection Lifecycle\n\nA connection progresses through the following states:\n\n```\nConnecting → Ready ──┬─→ Busy (at concurrent stream limit)\n                      │\n                      └─→ Draining (no more streams accepted, close after active streams finish)\n                           │\n                           └─→ Closed (queued for deletion)\n```\n\n**State Definitions**:\n- **Connecting**: TCP/TLS handshake in progress, `connect_timeout` applies\n- **ReadyForEarlyData** (HTTP/3 only): Ready to accept 0-RTT streams\n- **Ready**: Can accept additional streams immediately\n- **Busy**: Reached `max_concurrent_streams` limit (HTTP/2) or processing a stream (HTTP/1.1)\n- **Draining**: Received GOAWAY or circuit breaker triggered; closes after active streams complete\n- **Closed**: Connection destroyed, object deferred-deleted\n\n**Source**: `source/common/conn_pool/conn_pool_base.h:89-98`\n\n### HTTP/1.1 vs HTTP/2 Connection Differences\n\n#### HTTP/1.1 Pools\n- **One stream per connection** (multiplexing not supported)\n- `numActiveStreams()` returns 1 or 0 based on stream wrapper presence\n- Connection returns to `Ready` state only after stream completes (headers + body received)\n- State: `Connecting` → `Ready` → `Busy` (during stream) → `Ready` → `Draining`\n\n**Source**: `source/common/http/http1/conn_pool.h:28-34`\n\n#### HTTP/2 Pools\n- **Multiple streams per connection** (multiplexing)\n- `max_concurrent_streams` negotiated via HTTP/2 SETTINGS frame (can adjust after connection established)\n- Connection can accept new streams until concurrent stream limit reached\n- Sends GOAWAY to gracefully drain; actively transitions to `Draining` state\n- Receives peer SETTINGS; adjusts `concurrent_stream_limit_` down if needed\n\n**Source**: `source/common/http/conn_pool_base.cc:111-150` (onGoAway, onSettings handlers)\n\n### Per-Connection Configuration Limits\n\nEach active connection respects:\n- **`max_concurrent_streams`** (HTTP/2): Negotiated in handshake + SETTINGS updates\n- **`max_requests_per_connection`** (global): `host->cluster().maxRequestsPerConnection()`\n- **`remaining_streams_`**: Decrements with each stream; connection closes when 0 (or per-connection-buffer-limit reached)\n\n**Source**: `source/common/conn_pool/conn_pool_base.h:125-138`\n\n---\n\n## 2. Common Failure Scenarios\n\n### Scenario 1: Connection Pool Exhaustion (Pending Requests Overflow)\n\n**Symptom**: Clients see 503 errors; Envoy logs contain `\"max pending streams overflow\"`\n\n**Metrics to Check**:\n- `upstream_cx_overflow_` counter: Number of requests rejected due to pending overflow\n- `circuit_breakers.<cluster_name>.<priority>.cx_open_` gauge: Circuit breaker open (1 = open)\n- `circuit_breakers.<cluster_name>.<priority>.remaining_pending_` gauge: Remaining pending request capacity\n- `upstream_rq_pending_active_` gauge: Current pending streams in pool\n\n**Root Cause Analysis**:\n\nThis occurs when the number of in-flight requests exceeds `circuit_breakers.thresholds[].max_pending_requests`. The pool cannot create new connections fast enough or connections cannot drain pending requests quickly.\n\n```\nRequest arrives → Pool checks: canCreate(pending_requests)?\n                              ↓ No (at limit)\n                   → onPoolFailure(Overflow)\n                   → Reject request (503 + circuit_breaker_exceeded)\n```\n\n**Code Location**: `source/common/conn_pool/conn_pool_base.cc:346-350`\n\n**Diagnostic Steps**:\n\n1. **Check pending request circuit breaker status**:\n   ```bash\n   curl http://localhost:9901/stats/prometheus | grep 'circuit_breakers.*remaining_pending'\n   ```\n   Expected output (if open): `remaining_pending 0`\n\n2. **Check active pending streams**:\n   ```bash\n   curl http://localhost:9901/stats/prometheus | grep 'upstream_rq_pending_active'\n   ```\n   High value indicates backlog.\n\n3. **Examine cluster configuration**:\n   ```bash\n   curl http://localhost:9901/clusters | grep -A 20 '<cluster_name>'\n   ```\n   Look for `circuit_breakers` section, specifically `max_pending_requests`.\n\n4. **Check upstream response times** (slow backend):\n   ```bash\n   curl http://localhost:9901/stats/prometheus | grep 'upstream_rq_time'\n   ```\n   If `upstream_rq_time` histogram shows high latencies (mean/p99 >> 100ms), backend is slow.\n\n5. **Check for connection creation failures**:\n   ```bash\n   curl http://localhost:9901/stats/prometheus | grep 'upstream_cx_connect'\n   ```\n   High `upstream_cx_connect_fail` or `upstream_cx_connect_timeout` indicates cannot establish connections fast enough.\n\n**Configuration Fixes**:\n\n**Option A: Increase max_pending_requests**\n```yaml\nclusters:\n- name: my-cluster\n  circuit_breakers:\n    thresholds:\n    - priority: DEFAULT\n      max_pending_requests: 2048  # Increase from default 1024\n```\n⚠️ **Only if**: Temporary traffic spike; backend can handle more load.\n\n**Option B: Increase max_connections**\n```yaml\nclusters:\n- name: my-cluster\n  circuit_breakers:\n    thresholds:\n    - priority: DEFAULT\n      max_connections: 512  # Increase from default 100-200\n```\n- More connections = more concurrency; scales pending request handling.\n- Monitor resource consumption (memory, file descriptors).\n\n**Option C: Enable connection preconnection**\n```yaml\nclusters:\n- name: my-cluster\n  preconnect_policy:\n    num_initial_connections: 10\n    num_retries: 3\n```\n- Pre-establishes connections before requests arrive.\n- Reduces latency of new streams; mitigates pending overflow.\n\n**Option D: Reduce upstream latency**\n- Add caching at downstream proxy layer.\n- Optimize backend handler (database queries, external API calls).\n- Scale backend horizontally.\n\n---\n\n### Scenario 2: Upstream Connection Reset / Premature Close\n\n**Symptom**: Intermittent 503 errors; logs show `RemoteClose` or `LocalClose` events; high `upstream_cx_*` churn\n\n**Metrics to Check**:\n- `upstream_cx_total_` counter: Total connections created (high value = churn)\n- `upstream_cx_connect_fail_` counter: Failed connection attempts (TCP RST, refused)\n- `upstream_cx_rx_bytes_buffered_` vs `upstream_cx_rx_bytes_total_`: Data buffered/received\n- `upstream_rq_per_cx_` histogram: Requests per connection (low = short-lived)\n\n**Root Cause Analysis**:\n\nUpstream actively closes connections or connections fail before requests complete:\n\n1. **Backend resets TCP connection** (RST flag):\n   - Load balancer/firewall closing idle connections\n   - Backend overload (OOM, resource exhaustion)\n   - Connection timeout or keepalive expiry\n\n2. **TLS handshake failures**:\n   - Certificate validation errors\n   - TLS version mismatch\n   - SNI mismatch\n\n3. **HTTP/2 protocol violations**:\n   - Invalid HEADERS or DATA frames\n   - Stream ID exhaustion (rare)\n\n**Code Paths**:\n- `ActiveClient::onEvent(Network::ConnectionEvent::RemoteClose)` → `PoolFailureReason::RemoteConnectionFailure`\n- `ActiveClient::onEvent(Network::ConnectionEvent::LocalClose)` → `PoolFailureReason::LocalConnectionFailure`\n\n**Source**: `source/common/conn_pool/conn_pool_base.cc` and `source/common/tcp/conn_pool.cc:84-100`\n\n**Diagnostic Steps**:\n\n1. **Check connection count and failures**:\n   ```bash\n   curl http://localhost:9901/stats/prometheus | grep -E 'upstream_cx_(total|connect_fail|close|reset)'\n   ```\n   Interpret:\n   - `upstream_cx_total > 1000` per minute = high churn\n   - `upstream_cx_connect_fail / upstream_cx_total > 5%` = connection issues\n\n2. **Check TCP connection state**:\n   ```bash\n   # On proxy box, monitor upstream connections\n   netstat -antp | grep -E '<upstream_ip>:80|443' | wc -l\n   # Compare with expected (max_connections setting)\n   ```\n\n3. **Check for idle timeout on upstream**:\n   ```bash\n   # If seeing many connections but few requests, upstream likely closing idle\n   curl http://localhost:9901/stats/prometheus | grep 'upstream_rq_per_cx'\n   # Low values (1-2) suggest connections closing quickly\n   ```\n\n4. **Check Envoy's connection timeout configuration**:\n   ```bash\n   curl http://localhost:9901/config_dump | jq '.configs[] | select(.config_type==\"Cluster\")' | grep -E 'connect_timeout|tcp_keepalives'\n   ```\n\n5. **Check for TLS errors** (if using HTTPS upstream):\n   ```bash\n   tail -f /var/log/envoy/access.log | grep -i 'ssl\\|tls\\|certificate'\n   # Or check Envoy debug logs at WARN level\n   ```\n\n**Configuration Fixes**:\n\n**Option A: Increase connect_timeout (if TLS handshake slow)**\n```yaml\nclusters:\n- name: my-cluster\n  connect_timeout: 10s  # Default is 1s; increase for slow links\n```\n\n**Option B: Enable TCP keepalive**\n```yaml\nclusters:\n- name: my-cluster\n  upstream_connection_options:\n    tcp_keepalives:\n      keepalive_probes: 3\n      keepalive_interval: 10s\n      keepalive_time: 60s\n```\n- Prevents OS from closing idle TCP connections\n- Upstream sees regular keepalive packets\n\n**Option C: Disable per-connection request limit** (if requests per connection very low)\n```yaml\nclusters:\n- name: my-cluster\n  max_requests_per_connection: 0  # Unlimited\n  # or high value: 10000\n```\nConnections reuse for many requests.\n\n**Option D: Adjust pool idle timeout** (for TCP pools)\n```yaml\nclusters:\n- name: my-cluster\n  tcp_pool_idle_timeout: 10s  # Default likely higher\n```\nClose idle TCP connections proactively to reduce resource usage.\n\n**Option E: Check upstream load balancer settings**\n- Increase backend's `tcp_tw_reuse` (TIME_WAIT recycling)\n- Increase backend's max file descriptor limit\n- Check if upstream is actively rejecting connections (`netstat -s | grep 'rejected'`)\n\n---\n\n### Scenario 3: Circuit Breaker Triggering Unexpectedly\n\n**Symptom**: Large portion of traffic returning 503; circuit breaker stats show `cx_open_` = 1; no obvious upstream issues\n\n**Metrics to Check**:\n- `circuit_breakers.<cluster>.<priority>.cx_open_` : 1 = open, 0 = closed\n- `circuit_breakers.<cluster>.<priority>.remaining_*` gauges (connections, pending_requests, requests)\n- `upstream_cx_total_` : total connections (should equal `max_connections` if breaker open)\n\n**Root Cause Analysis**:\n\nThe resource manager prevents new connections/requests before the pool actually reaches capacity. This can happen due to:\n\n1. **Transient traffic spike**: Spike exceeds threshold momentarily\n2. **Misconfigured limits**: `max_connections` set too low for actual traffic\n3. **Slow backend**: Connections held open longer; new requests blocked\n4. **Asymmetric configuration**: Multiple Envoy proxies competing for shared upstream; each proxy's limit too low\n\n**Code Flow**:\n```\nnewStream() called\n  → parent.host().resourceManager().pendingRequests().canCreate()?\n  → if No: onPoolFailure(Overflow, ...) // Not ConnectionFailure\n```\n\n**Source**: `source/common/conn_pool/conn_pool_base.cc:346-350`\n\n**Diagnostic Steps**:\n\n1. **Confirm circuit breaker is actually open**:\n   ```bash\n   curl http://localhost:9901/stats/prometheus | grep 'circuit_breakers.*\\.cx_open_' | grep ' 1$'\n   # If > 0, breaker is open\n   ```\n\n2. **Check remaining capacity**:\n   ```bash\n   curl http://localhost:9901/stats/prometheus | grep 'remaining_' | grep 'circuit'\n   # Look for remaining_connections_*, remaining_pending_*\n   # If 0, threshold reached\n   ```\n\n3. **Check current vs max**:\n   ```bash\n   # Get max_connections setting\n   curl http://localhost:9901/clusters | grep -A 30 '<cluster_name>' | grep -i 'max.*connection'\n\n   # Count current active connections\n   curl http://localhost:9901/stats/prometheus | grep 'upstream_cx_total'\n   ```\n   If `upstream_cx_total >= max_connections`: Expected behavior, breaker should open.\n\n4. **Check if traffic pattern changed**:\n   ```bash\n   # Look at request rate and latency\n   curl http://localhost:9901/stats/prometheus | grep 'upstream_rq_' | grep -E '(time|total)'\n   ```\n\n5. **Check for slow requests**:\n   ```bash\n   # High mean/p99 latency = requests held longer = fewer concurrent capacity\n   curl http://localhost:9901/stats/prometheus | grep 'upstream_rq_time'\n   ```\n\n**Configuration Fixes**:\n\n**Option A: Increase max_connections**\n```yaml\nclusters:\n- name: my-cluster\n  circuit_breakers:\n    thresholds:\n    - priority: DEFAULT\n      max_connections: 512  # Increase from, e.g., 100\n```\nMust be balanced with resource (memory, file descriptors, RAM per host).\n\n**Option B: Increase per-host limits** (if using load balancing with multiple hosts)\n```yaml\nclusters:\n- name: my-cluster\n  common_http_protocol_options:\n    max_connections_per_host: 50  # Distribute connections across hosts\n  circuit_breakers:\n    thresholds:\n    - priority: DEFAULT\n      max_connections: 200  # Lower global limit OK if spread per-host\n```\n\n**Option C: Reduce request timeout**\n```yaml\nclusters:\n- name: my-cluster\n  timeout: 5s  # Shorter timeout = requests complete faster = more capacity\n```\nOnly if requests can realistically complete in time.\n\n**Option D: Add retries with exponential backoff** (at router level)\n```yaml\nvirtual_hosts:\n- name: my_vhost\n  routes:\n  - match:\n      prefix: /api\n    route:\n      cluster: my-cluster\n      retry_policy:\n        num_retries: 3\n        retry_host_predicate:\n        - name: envoy.retry_host_predicates.previous_hosts\n```\nAllows requests to retry against other backends if first attempt hits circuit breaker.\n\n**Option E: Monitor and alert on circuit breaker status**\n```yaml\n# Add metric watch\n# Alert when circuit_breakers.<cluster>.*.cx_open_ == 1 for > 10s\n```\n\n---\n\n### Scenario 4: HTTP/2 GOAWAY Causing Request Failures\n\n**Symptom**: Spike of 503 errors or stream resets; logs show upstream `GOAWAY` frame; requests fail with `RemoteReset` or `ConnectionTermination` reason\n\n**Metrics to Check**:\n- `upstream_cx_close_notify_` counter: Number of GOAWAY frames received\n- `upstream_rq_reset_` gauge: Active request resets\n- `upstream_rq_per_cx_` histogram: Drops sharply when GOAWAY sent\n\n**Root Cause Analysis**:\n\nHTTP/2 server sends GOAWAY frame when:\n1. **Graceful shutdown**: Server shutting down; tells clients to use other connections\n2. **Connection duration limit**: Server enforces max connection lifetime\n3. **Stream ID exhaustion**: Rare; 2^31 stream IDs consumed (millions of streams)\n4. **Protocol violation**: Invalid frame, stream reset, flow control violation\n5. **Resource constraint**: Memory pressure, too many streams\n\nWhen upstream sends GOAWAY:\n- All **in-flight streams on that connection are reset** (or complete if headers already sent)\n- Connection transitions to `Draining` state\n- No new streams assigned to connection\n- Connection closes after all active streams complete\n\n**Code Flow**:\n```cpp\nvoid MultiplexedActiveClientBase::onGoAway(Http::GoAwayErrorCode) {\n  // Line 112: Log debug message\n  // Line 113: Increment upstream_cx_close_notify_\n  if (numActiveRequests() == 0) {\n    close();  // No active streams, close immediately\n  } else {\n    transitionActiveClientState(*this, ActiveClient::State::Draining);  // Wait for streams to finish\n  }\n}\n```\n\n**Source**: `source/common/http/conn_pool_base.cc:111-121`\n\n**Diagnostic Steps**:\n\n1. **Confirm GOAWAY is being sent**:\n   ```bash\n   curl http://localhost:9901/stats/prometheus | grep 'upstream_cx_close_notify'\n   # If > 0, GOAWAYs are happening\n   ```\n\n2. **Timestamp of GOAWAY events**:\n   ```bash\n   # Tail envoy debug logs if available\n   tail -f /var/log/envoy/debug.log | grep -i 'goaway'\n   ```\n\n3. **Check active streams before/after**:\n   ```bash\n   # Monitor in real-time during incident\n   watch 'curl -s http://localhost:9901/stats/prometheus | grep -E \"upstream_cx|upstream_rq_active\"'\n   ```\n\n4. **Check upstream server logs for shutdown/scaling signals**:\n   ```bash\n   # On upstream service, check logs\n   tail -f /var/log/app/server.log | grep -i 'shutdown\\|drain\\|goaway'\n   ```\n\n5. **Check HTTP/2 settings negotiation**:\n   ```bash\n   curl http://localhost:9901/config_dump | jq '.configs[] | select(.config_type==\"Cluster\") | .config' | grep -i 'h2\\|http2'\n   ```\n\n**Configuration Fixes**:\n\n**Option A: Accept GOAWAY gracefully with retries**\n```yaml\n# At route level: enable retries to other connections/backends\nvirtual_hosts:\n- name: my_vhost\n  routes:\n  - match:\n      prefix: /\n    route:\n      cluster: my-cluster\n      retry_policy:\n        num_retries: 1\n        retry_on: reset  # Retry on connection reset/GOAWAY\n        per_try_timeout: 2s\n```\n\n**Option B: Reduce max_requests_per_connection** (if upstream has low limit)\n```yaml\nclusters:\n- name: my-cluster\n  max_requests_per_connection: 1000  # Gracefully close before upstream GOAWAY\n```\nPro-actively close Envoy-side connections to avoid GOAWAY surprise.\n\n**Option C: Increase idle timeout** (if upstream GOAWAYs idle connections)\n```yaml\nclusters:\n- name: my-cluster\n  http2_protocol_options:\n    connection_idle_timeout: 120s  # Increase from default\n```\n\n**Option D: Coordinate with upstream on shutdown**\n```yaml\n# Ensure upstream sends GOAWAY before accepting new connections\n# Document: \"When scaling down, send GOAWAY 30s before accepting no new connections\"\n# Envoy will move conn to Draining; backoff new streams to other upstream\n```\n\n**Option E: Monitor and alert**\n```yaml\n# Alert when upstream_cx_close_notify_ increases rapidly\n# Possible actions: auto-scale up downstream capacity, drain traffic to other upstreams\n```\n\n---\n\n## 3. Diagnostic Commands\n\n### Key Envoy Admin API Endpoints\n\n#### `/stats` (or `/stats/prometheus`)\nReturns all stats in Prometheus format. Useful for scripting.\n\n```bash\n# Get all connection pool stats for a cluster\ncurl http://localhost:9901/stats/prometheus | grep 'cluster\\.my_cluster'\n\n# Get circuit breaker status\ncurl http://localhost:9901/stats/prometheus | grep 'circuit_breaker'\n\n# Get HTTP/1 vs HTTP/2 specific metrics\ncurl http://localhost:9901/stats/prometheus | grep 'upstream_cx'\n```\n\n#### `/clusters`\nLists all clusters and their status (human-readable).\n\n```bash\ncurl http://localhost:9901/clusters | grep -A 30 'my_cluster'\n\n# Output includes:\n# - Circuit breakers thresholds\n# - Current connections\n# - Load balancer status\n# - Hosts/endpoints\n```\n\n#### `/config_dump`\nDumps the entire Envoy configuration (listeners, routes, clusters). JSON format.\n\n```bash\n# Dump cluster config\ncurl http://localhost:9901/config_dump | jq '.configs[] | select(.config_type==\"Cluster\") | select(.config.name==\"my_cluster\")'\n\n# Check circuit breaker config\ncurl http://localhost:9901/config_dump | jq '.configs[] | select(.config_type==\"Cluster\") | .config.circuit_breakers'\n```\n\n#### `/stats/histogram_bucket` (if available)\nBreaks down histogram values (e.g., `upstream_rq_time`) into buckets.\n\n```bash\ncurl http://localhost:9901/stats/histogram_bucket/upstream_rq_time\n```\n\n### Key Metrics for Connection Pool Diagnosis\n\n| Metric | Type | Meaning |\n|--------|------|---------|\n| `upstream_cx_total` | Counter | Total connections created |\n| `upstream_cx_overflow` | Counter | Connections rejected due to max circuit breaker |\n| `upstream_cx_connect_fail` | Counter | Failed TCP/TLS handshakes |\n| `upstream_cx_connect_timeout` | Counter | Connections timing out (exceed `connect_timeout`) |\n| `upstream_cx_close_notify` | Counter | Received GOAWAY (HTTP/2) or similar |\n| `upstream_rq_pending_total` | Counter | Total requests queued (ever) |\n| `upstream_rq_pending_active` | Gauge | Current pending requests |\n| `upstream_rq_per_cx` | Histogram | Requests completed per connection |\n| `upstream_rq_time` | Histogram | Request latency (downstream→upstream→downstream) |\n| `circuit_breakers.<cluster>.<priority>.cx_open_` | Gauge | 1 = circuit breaker open, 0 = closed |\n| `circuit_breakers.<cluster>.<priority>.remaining_*` | Gauge | Remaining capacity (connections, requests, pending) |\n\n### Example Diagnostic Session\n\n```bash\n# Step 1: Check overall cluster health\ncurl http://localhost:9901/clusters | grep my_cluster\n\n# Step 2: Check if circuit breaker is open\ncurl http://localhost:9901/stats/prometheus | grep 'circuit_breakers.*my_cluster.*cx_open'\n\n# Step 3: If open, check remaining capacity\ncurl http://localhost:9901/stats/prometheus | grep 'circuit_breakers.*my_cluster.*remaining'\n\n# Step 4: Check connection churn\ncurl http://localhost:9901/stats/prometheus | grep 'my_cluster.*upstream_cx_' | head -20\n\n# Step 5: Check request latency\ncurl http://localhost:9901/stats/prometheus | grep 'my_cluster.*upstream_rq_time'\n\n# Step 6: Dump config to verify settings\ncurl http://localhost:9901/config_dump | jq '.configs[] | select(.config.name==\"my_cluster\") | .config.circuit_breakers'\n```\n\n---\n\n## 4. Configuration Fixes and Tuning\n\n### Circuit Breaker Thresholds\n\n```yaml\nclusters:\n- name: my_cluster\n  circuit_breakers:\n    thresholds:\n    # DEFAULT priority (normal traffic)\n    - priority: DEFAULT\n      max_connections: 100\n      max_pending_requests: 100\n      max_requests: 100\n      max_retries: 3\n      track_remaining: true  # Export remaining_* stats\n    # HIGH priority (e.g., health checks, admin)\n    - priority: HIGH\n      max_connections: 10\n      max_pending_requests: 10\n      max_requests: 10\n      max_retries: 1\n```\n\n**Tuning Guidelines**:\n- **`max_connections`**: Typically `min(10, num_upstream_instances) * num_proxy_threads`\n  - If upstream has 4 instances and proxy has 8 worker threads: `10 * 8 = 80` per cluster\n  - Verify against resource limits (file descriptors, memory)\n- **`max_pending_requests`**: Usually `2–5x max_connections` to allow request queueing\n- **`max_requests`**: Usually same as `max_connections` to prevent overwhelming upstream\n- **`max_retries`**: Usually 3–5; may be 1 if retries happen at outer layer\n\n**Runtime Override** (for dynamic tuning):\n```yaml\n# In runtime_config.yaml or via runtime overrides\nruntime_values:\n  overrides:\n  - resource_key: \"circuit_breakers.my_cluster.default.max_connections\"\n    value: 200\n```\n\n### Connection Timeout and Keepalive\n\n```yaml\nclusters:\n- name: my_cluster\n  # TCP connection establishment timeout\n  connect_timeout: 2s  # Default 1s; increase for high-latency links (satellite, WAN)\n\n  # TCP keepalive for long-lived connections\n  upstream_connection_options:\n    tcp_keepalives:\n      keepalive_probes: 3         # TCP_KEEPCNT\n      keepalive_interval: 10s     # TCP_KEEPINTVL\n      keepalive_time: 300s        # TCP_KEEPIDLE (5 minutes)\n```\n\n**When to adjust**:\n- `connect_timeout > 1s`: When upstream is geographically distant or has slow TLS handshake\n- `tcp_keepalives`: When connections idle for extended periods; prevents intermediary (firewall, LB) from closing\n\n### Per-Connection Limits\n\n```yaml\nclusters:\n- name: my_cluster\n  # Max requests per connection before closing and opening new\n  max_requests_per_connection: 0  # 0 = unlimited (default); set to positive integer to limit\n\n  # HTTP/2 specific: max concurrent streams\n  http2_protocol_options:\n    max_concurrent_streams: 100   # Negotiated via SETTINGS frame\n    initial_stream_window_size: 65536  # Default 64KiB\n    initial_connection_window_size: 1048576  # Default 1MiB\n```\n\n**Tuning**:\n- `max_requests_per_connection`: Set to gracefully recycle connections (e.g., 10,000) if upstream has per-connection memory leaks\n- `max_concurrent_streams` (HTTP/2): If upstream advertises lower value, Envoy respects it. Override only if upstream value is too conservative.\n\n### Buffer Limits\n\n```yaml\nclusters:\n- name: my_cluster\n  # Max bytes buffered per upstream connection (for pending data)\n  per_connection_buffer_limit_bytes: 32768  # Default 32KiB\n\n  # Useful when upstream has slow write socket buffer or Envoy has memory constraints\n```\n\n**When to adjust**:\n- Decrease if proxying large request bodies and memory is limited\n- Increase if upstream has high RTT and benefits from buffering\n\n### Preconnection\n\n```yaml\nclusters:\n- name: my_cluster\n  preconnect_policy:\n    # Pre-establish N connections when pool is created\n    num_initial_connections: 5\n    # Number of additional connections to attempt if preconnect incomplete\n    num_retries: 3\n```\n\n**Effect**: Reduces latency of first request by pre-warming connection pool.\n\n### Example: High-Throughput Configuration\n\n```yaml\nclusters:\n- name: high_throughput_backend\n  connect_timeout: 3s  # TLS handshake can be slow\n\n  circuit_breakers:\n    thresholds:\n    - priority: DEFAULT\n      max_connections: 500  # Scale up for high throughput\n      max_pending_requests: 1000\n      max_requests: 500\n      max_retries: 5\n      track_remaining: true\n\n  http2_protocol_options:\n    max_concurrent_streams: 100\n    initial_connection_window_size: 2097152  # 2 MiB for large request bodies\n\n  upstream_connection_options:\n    tcp_keepalives:\n      keepalive_time: 60s\n      keepalive_interval: 10s\n      keepalive_probes: 3\n\n  max_requests_per_connection: 10000  # Recycle after 10k requests to prevent leaks\n\n  preconnect_policy:\n    num_initial_connections: 10\n    num_retries: 3\n```\n\n---\n\n## 5. Code References\n\n### Key Source Files and Functions\n\n#### Base Connection Pool (Shared Logic)\n- **File**: `source/common/conn_pool/conn_pool_base.h`\n  - `class ConnPoolImplBase`: Base pool implementation\n  - `class ActiveClient`: Base active connection representation\n  - `class PendingStream`: Queued request awaiting connection\n\n- **File**: `source/common/conn_pool/conn_pool_base.cc`\n  - `ConnPoolImplBase::newStreamImpl()`: Main entry point for new streams\n  - `ConnPoolImplBase::tryCreateNewConnections()`: Attempt to establish connections\n  - `ConnPoolImplBase::onConnectionEvent()`: Handle TCP/TLS events\n  - `PendingStream::PendingStream()`: Constructor; increments pending request count\n\n#### HTTP Connection Pool\n- **File**: `source/common/http/conn_pool_base.h`\n  - `class HttpConnPoolImplBase`: HTTP pool base (shared by HTTP/1.1 and HTTP/2)\n  - `class ActiveClient`: HTTP-specific active client\n  - `class MultiplexedActiveClientBase`: Base for HTTP/2 and HTTP/3 (multiplexed)\n\n- **File**: `source/common/http/conn_pool_base.cc`\n  - `MultiplexedActiveClientBase::onGoAway()`: **Handle HTTP/2 GOAWAY**\n  - `MultiplexedActiveClientBase::onSettings()`: **Handle HTTP/2 SETTINGS (max_concurrent_streams)**\n\n#### HTTP/1.1 Connection Pool\n- **File**: `source/common/http/http1/conn_pool.h`\n  - `class ActiveClient`: HTTP/1.1-specific active client\n  - `struct StreamWrapper`: Wraps request/response encoder/decoder pair\n\n- **File**: `source/common/http/http1/conn_pool.cc`\n  - HTTP/1.1 codec client instantiation\n\n#### HTTP/2 Connection Pool\n- **File**: `source/common/http/http2/conn_pool.h`\n  - `class ActiveClient`: HTTP/2-specific active client (inherits from `MultiplexedActiveClientBase`)\n\n- **File**: `source/common/http/http2/conn_pool.cc`\n  - HTTP/2 codec client instantiation\n  - SETTINGS frame handling\n\n#### TCP Connection Pool\n- **File**: `source/common/tcp/conn_pool.h`\n  - `class ConnPoolImpl`: TCP pool implementation\n  - `class ActiveTcpClient`: TCP active client\n\n- **File**: `source/common/tcp/conn_pool.cc`\n  - `ActiveTcpClient::onEvent()`: Handle TCP connection events\n  - `ActiveTcpClient::onIdleTimeout()`: Close idle TCP connections\n\n#### Circuit Breaker and Resource Management\n- **File**: `source/common/upstream/upstream_impl.h`\n  - `class ClusterInfoImpl::CircuitBreakerManager`: Manages resource thresholds\n\n- **File**: `source/common/upstream/upstream_impl.cc`\n  - `CircuitBreakerManager::CircuitBreakerManager()`: Initialize thresholds from config\n  - Resource increment/decrement logic\n\n### Tracing Pool Failures\n\nWhen diagnosing a pool failure, trace these code paths:\n\n**For Overflow (pending request rejected)**:\n1. `ConnPoolImplBase::newStreamImpl()` (line 259, base header)\n2. Check `resourceManager().pendingRequests().canCreate()` (upstream_impl.cc:347)\n3. Call `onPoolFailure(..., PoolFailureReason::Overflow, ...)` (upstream_impl.cc:349)\n\n**For Connection Failure (TCP RST/timeout)**:\n1. `ActiveClient::onEvent(Network::ConnectionEvent::RemoteClose)` or `LocalClose`\n2. Call `parent_.onConnectionEvent(*this, failureReason, event)` (conn_pool_base.cc:158)\n3. Call `onPoolFailure(..., PoolFailureReason::RemoteConnectionFailure/LocalConnectionFailure, ...)`\n\n**For HTTP/2 GOAWAY**:\n1. HTTP/2 codec receives GOAWAY frame\n2. Call `MultiplexedActiveClientBase::onGoAway(...)` (conn_pool_base.cc:111)\n3. Transition to `Draining` state (line 118)\n4. Drain remaining streams; close connection\n\n---\n\n## Appendix: Runtime Tuning Command Examples\n\n### Check Current Settings\n```bash\n# SSH to Envoy proxy\n$ ssh envoy-proxy.example.com\n\n# Query stats endpoint\n$ curl http://localhost:9901/clusters | grep -A 50 \"my_cluster\"\n$ curl http://localhost:9901/stats/prometheus | grep 'circuit_breakers.*my_cluster'\n```\n\n### Enable Debug Logging for Connection Pool\n```bash\n# At startup, set log level\nenvoy -l debug --config-path /etc/envoy.yaml\n\n# Or patch config at runtime (if admin API supports)\ncurl -X POST http://localhost:9901/logging?...  # Depends on Envoy version\n```\n\n### Monitor in Real-Time\n```bash\n# Watch pool stats every second\nwatch -n 1 \"curl -s http://localhost:9901/stats/prometheus | grep -E 'upstream_cx_|pending|circuit'\"\n\n# Or with jq for JSON prettification\nwatch -n 1 \"curl -s http://localhost:9901/config_dump | jq '.configs[] | select(.config_type==\\\"Cluster\\\") | select(.config.name==\\\"my_cluster\\\") | .config.circuit_breakers'\"\n```\n\n### Adjust Circuit Breaker via Config\nEdit `/etc/envoy/envoy.yaml`, update thresholds, and trigger config reload:\n```bash\n# HUP signal reloads config (graceful)\n$ kill -HUP $(pidof envoy)\n\n# Verify new settings applied\n$ curl http://localhost:9901/clusters | grep -A 50 \"my_cluster\"\n```\n\n---\n\n## Summary\n\nEnvoy connection pools are the critical path for upstream communication. Most production issues stem from:\n\n1. **Insufficient capacity** (circuit breakers too low)\n2. **Connection churn** (upstream closing, TLS failures, timeouts)\n3. **Slow backends** (pending request backlog)\n4. **Configuration mismatch** (Envoy limits vs. upstream capabilities)\n\nUse the diagnostic steps in **Section 3** to identify root cause, then apply fixes from **Sections 2 and 4**. Monitor metrics in **Section 3** to validate improvements.\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
